Now : 2017-01-25 13:44:24.  Time  :
SELECT `users`.*, `groups`.`description` as `user_group_description`, GROUP_CONCAT(clients.client_name ) as client_name
FROM `users`
LEFT JOIN `users_groups` ON `users_groups`.`user_id` = `users`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `groups` ON `groups`.`id` = `users_groups`.`group_id`
LEFT JOIN `users_clients` ON `users_clients`.`uc_user_id` = `users`.`id` AND `users_clients`.`uc_active_status` in ('E','O')
LEFT JOIN `clients` ON `clients`.`cid` = `users_clients`.`uc_client_id`
GROUP BY `users`.`id`, `groups`.`description`
ORDER BY `username`
 LIMIT 10

JOIN `users_groups` ON `users_groups`.`user_id` = `users`.`id`
JOIN `groups` ON `groups`.`id` = `users_groups`.`group_id`
WHERE `users`.`id` = '1'
